\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
Michael\textquotesingle{}s lock-\/free ordered single-\/linked list (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}%
 Usually, ordered single-\/linked list is used as a building block for the hash table implementation. The complexity of searching is {\ttfamily O(\+N)}.

Template arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type to be stored in the list; the type {\ttfamily T} should be based on (or has a member of type) cds\+::intrusive\+::micheal\+\_\+list\+::node
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1michael__list_1_1traits}{michael\+\_\+list\+::traits}} for explanation. It is possible to declare option-\/based list with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1michael__list_1_1make__traits}{cds\+::intrusive\+::michael\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction, see \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{here} for explanations.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Usage}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{intrusive_2michael__list__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/michael\+\_\+list\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files. For example, for \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01general__buffered_3_01_buffer_00_01_lock_00_01_backoff_01_4_01_4_cds_urcu_general_buffered_gc}{general-\/purpose buffered RCU} you should include\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\_buffered.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{intrusive_2michael__list__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/michael\_list\_rcu.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Now,\ you\ can\ declare\ Michael's\ list\ for\ type\ Foo\ and\ default\ traits:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds::intrusive::MichaelList<cds::urcu::gc<\ cds::urcu::general\_buffered<>}}\ >,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Foo}}\ >\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{rcu\_michael\_list}};}

Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for Michael\textquotesingle{}s list has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item to protect the value, the iterator contains a GC-\/specific guard + another guard is required locally for increment operator. For some GC (like as {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1gc_af0523881f089593a7559d194ee2b5dd9}{gc\+::\+HP}}), a guard is a limited resource per thread, so an exception (or assertion) "{}no free guard"{} may be thrown if the limit of guard count per thread is exceeded.
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary since it contains thread-\/private GC\textquotesingle{}s guard.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item the iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations there is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\end{DoxyWarning}

Forward iterator 

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the item the iterator points to. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_ad437d91c4fbd4352b9f5a682913acc9e}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!key\_comparator@{key\_comparator}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::clear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Clears the list using default disposer 

The function clears the list using default (provided by {\ttfamily Traits} class template argument) disposer functor.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} invocation can be deferred.

The function can throw {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock}} exception if a deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. 函数调用图\+:

Checks whether the list contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a00d678026b04d3e10064a461360b2dc8}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

Do not use the value returned by {\ttfamily end} function to access any item. Internally, {\ttfamily end} returning value equals to {\ttfamily nullptr}.

The returned value can be used only to control reaching the end of the list. \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item.

The function can throw \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock_cds_urcu_rcu_deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock} exception if a deadlock is detected and the deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a69068e4efbafb30996ed73330dc6ddcd}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}
\index{erase@{erase}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a69068e4efbafb30996ed73330dc6ddcd} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, call {\ttfamily func} functor with item found, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}, {\ttfamily func} is not called.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aeb3ef2856d90adde37e021f1204598e8}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}
\index{erase@{erase}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aeb3ef2856d90adde37e021f1204598e8} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, call {\ttfamily func} functor with item found, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item.

The function can throw \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock_cds_urcu_rcu_deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock} exception if a deadlock is detected and the deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a0346b37037e540fd06803edc9137158d}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}
\index{erase\_with@{erase\_with}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase\_with()}{erase\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a0346b37037e540fd06803edc9137158d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_erase_val}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_adf2e8c008551a72f8ab260e30303c082}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aeb3ef2856d90adde37e021f1204598e8}{erase(\+Q const\&, Func)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list.

Extracts the item from the list with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key}, unlinks it from the list, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a672ecef002dff123b37d09f39e2ba52a} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afdaf86ddeed6c527562b64442cec476f}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, unlinks it from the list, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afdaf86ddeed6c527562b64442cec476f}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The function does NOT dispose the item found. It just unlinks the item from the list and returns a pointer to item found. You shouldn\textquotesingle{}t lock RCU for current thread before calling this function, and you should manually release the returned exempt pointer before reusing it.
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts the item using compare functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a7b1c519045e7079e82852be15c126fc2}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_with()}{extract\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a7b1c519045e7079e82852be15c126fc2} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afdaf86ddeed6c527562b64442cec476f}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

This function is the analog for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a672ecef002dff123b37d09f39e2ba52a}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} 

The {\ttfamily pred} is a predicate used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a372e125b70c8cb1637d540d4c448c69e}{key\+\_\+comparator}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_ac3a9121f2eb5e73ccd40a56a0ccfe17a}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}
\index{find@{find}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find()}{find()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_ac3a9121f2eb5e73ccd40a56a0ccfe17a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} in the list 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the function is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The function does not serialize simultaneous access to the {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema to keep out unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily key} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor may modify both arguments.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aff819d0ab63437fa790adf139eeaa66f}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}
\index{find@{find}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find()}{find()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aff819d0ab63437fa790adf139eeaa66f} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



\doxylink{struct_find}{Find} the key {\ttfamily val} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. The function {\ttfamily find} does not serialize simultaneous access to the list {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The function makes RCU lock internally.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

Finds the {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_find_func}{find(Q\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aee0f0ccfc0f0dc8f13b1288f317da96f}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find\_with@{find\_with}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a890da1fb3f5022ad4b5707698b4b5ae1}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} object.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a3300d19ae0e5c427265da83658e2bcbf} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a29215283ae0a9fdd0bd2e1dfb7a40def}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp_get}{get( Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad1ff656bb247fb88251980d1d1e522bb}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_with()}{get\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad1ff656bb247fb88251980d1d1e522bb} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a890da1fb3f5022ad4b5707698b4b5ae1}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a272011bc98e96b3ea372c12e28147f26}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a272011bc98e96b3ea372c12e28147f26} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} into the list if the list does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} has been linked to the list, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af1c5cc5d6d6bc91ea68d554be0aad682}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the list if the list does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

The function makes RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is linked into the list, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_af607e26bd35e38999b66d7786e305e1c}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_af607e26bd35e38999b66d7786e305e1c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split new item creating into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the list
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this list\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split new item creating into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the list
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this list\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

The function makes RCU lock internally.

size\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{\+::size}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns list\textquotesingle{}s item count 

The value returned depends on item counter provided by {\ttfamily Traits}. For {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter}}, this function always returns 0.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even if you use real item counter and it returns 0, this fact does not mean that the list is empty. To check list emptiness use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2da555d3b4fe15d357fda0fbd5b8f7bf}{empty()}} method. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a91c09fdf39280401d1b9c37cea532ebd}{stat}} const  \& \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::statistics (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns const reference to internal statistics 

\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_af9e33214594355484bb5a7b0051a7b1c}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_af9e33214594355484bb5a7b0051a7b1c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the list 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the list and unlinks it from the list if it is found and it is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1872225178895b7b1ea4b3e1f7b5da73}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}()\+: {\ttfamily erase}() finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of the list, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae97d60a65dae617946ec4b26df587083}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}
\index{unlink@{unlink}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae97d60a65dae617946ec4b26df587083} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the list 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the list and unlink it from the list if it is found and it is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1872225178895b7b1ea4b3e1f7b5da73}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}() functions\+: {\ttfamily erase}() finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of that list, i.\+e. the pointer to the item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48f21897d7193ebd62827e7f8545b3cf}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for unlinked item.

The function can throw \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock} exception if deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a95e54e2714eb2d6d73d225a329c5dc9f}\index{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::MichaelList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a95e54e2714eb2d6d73d225a329c5dc9f} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the item 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} not found in the list, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the list iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the list
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a95e54e2714eb2d6d73d225a329c5dc9f}{update()}} function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the list.

The function makes RCU lock internally.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_a5ca6c8d0948a29705ffa7e6b5123fa2b} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Michael\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the list, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65e058e6721e4a81a6ab5fdd943bcf98}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the list
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a95e54e2714eb2d6d73d225a329c5dc9f}{update()}} function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refers to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with that key already in the list.

See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}
